
#Important to put HIGHEST first
GER_mefo_bills_level_up = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_22 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_22
			add_idea = GER_mefo_bills_23
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_21 }

#Important to put HIGHEST first
GER_remove_mefo_bills = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_1 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_1
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_2 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_2
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_3 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_3
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_4 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_4
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_5 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_5
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_6 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_6
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_7 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_7
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_8 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_8
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_9 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_9
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_10 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_10
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_11 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_11
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_12 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_12
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_13 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_13
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_14 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_14
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_15 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_15
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_16 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_16
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_17 }

	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_18 }

	else_if = {

	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_20 }

# Like the level up effect except it runs in reverse
# For use when annexing the gold reserves of Austria, Czechoslovakia and Yugoslavia

GER_mefo_bills_level_down = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_1 }
		remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_1
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_2
			add_idea = GER_mefo_bills_1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_3
			add_idea = GER_mefo_bills_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_4 }

			remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_4

		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_5 }

			remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_5

GER_atlantik_wall_level_up = {

				has_idea = GER_atlanticc_wall_0000
			}
		}

			remove_idea = GER_atlanticc_wall_0000
			add_idea = GER_atlanticc_wall_0000kurwa

			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
			}

GER_war_zone_scripted_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			GER = {
				has_war_with = SOV 
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = GER_war_zone_flag
				OR = {
					is_fully_controlled_by = GER
					is_fully_controlled_by = ROM  
					is_fully_controlled_by = HUN 
					is_fully_controlled_by = BUL 
					is_fully_controlled_by = SLO 
					is_fully_controlled_by = ITA 
					is_fully_controlled_by = SPR 
					is_fully_controlled_by = EFR 
				}	
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_war_zone_modifier }
			set_state_flag = GER_war_zone_flag_set_flag
		}
	}
}
GER_war_zone_scripted_effect_down = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			GER = {
				has_war_with = SOV 
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = GER_war_zone_flag
				is_fully_controlled_by = SOV
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_war_zone_modifier }
			set_state_flag = GER_war_zone_flag_set_flag
		}
	}
}
GER_economy_of_plunder = {
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_5 
			}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_5
			add_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_4 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_4
			add_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_3
			add_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_2
			add_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_1
			add_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_2
		}		
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_1 } }
		add_ideas = GER_economy_of_plunder_1
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_idea = GER_economy_of_plunder_1 } }
		add_ideas = GER_economy_of_plunder_1
	}
}
